## Memory Allocator


| memory_clear |
|---|
| **Description:** - **Command.** Clears the video memory, ffp buffer and memory pools, deletes textures and all meshes, including skinned meshes and decals. Memory is cleared automatically after the world is loaded or the render preset has been changed. It is recommended to use this command only in case a significant amount of memory needs to be released, the resources will be force removed at the end of the frame. |
| memory_clear_soft |
| **Description:** - **Command.** Softly clears the video memory. Destroys unused textures and meshes and clears memory pools. |


### RAM Allocations


Operations on memory allocations.

| memory_info |  |
|---|---|
| **Description:** - **Command.** Prints [information](../../principles/allocator/index.md#analyze_ram_pools) on small allocations in the static and dynamic memory pools. |  |
| memory_statistics_enabled | Config file: [*.boot](../../code/configuration_file_cpp.md#boot) |
| **Description:** - **Variable.**   Prints a value indicating if the option controlled by the command below is enabled. - **Command.**   Enables gathering memory statistics during the application start-up. After starting up prints the value indicating whether gathering memory statistics is enabled or not. > **Notice:** Available only during the Engine initialization (startup), has no effect at run time. | **Arguments:** **0** - disabled **1** - enabled (by default) |
| memory_optimize_static_pools |  |
| **Description:** - **Command.** Updates and optimizes the static memory pools. The command can receive three arguments. | **Arguments:** - ***by_default*** - a flag indicating if the pool will be optimized for all the platforms or it will be customized for the current binary executable. To optimize pools for the current platform according to the current configuration, pass false. This way you can create several configurations of the static pools for different platforms. The default value is true. - ***overflow*** - a permissible difference between the maximum potential memory consumption and the current memory consumption. This value can be useful for reducing allocations during memory spikes. When set to 0, it generates the static pools based on current memory consumption. The default value is 64 Mb. - ***max_size*** - the maximum size of all static pools. The default value is 8192 Mb. |
| memory_dynamic_pool |  |
| **Description:** - **Variable.** Sets the maximum size of the dynamic pool in bytes. - **Command.** Prints the maximum size of the dynamic pool in bytes. | **Arguments:** Pool size in bytes. 256 by default. |


### VRAM Allocations


For more details about heap types, please refer to [this article](https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/windows/win32/api/d3d12/ne-d3d12-d3d12_heap_type).


Operations on video memory allocations.

| video_memory_info |  |
|---|---|
| **Description:** - **Command.** Prints [information](../../principles/allocator/index.md#analyze_vram_pools) on small video memory allocations. |  |
| d3d12_small_pool_enabled |  |
| **Description:** - **Variable.** Toggles small pool allocations on and off. You should call the [`boot_config_save`](#boot_config_save) command and restart the application to save and apply changes. - **Command.** Prints the value indicating whether small pool allocations are enabled or not. | **Arguments:** - 0 to disable allocations - 1 to enable allocations |
| d3d12_gpu_upload_heap |  |
| **Description:** - **Variable.**   Prints a value indicating if the option controlled by the command below is enabled. - **Command.**    Enables the use of a persistent GPU upload heap for staging data from CPU to GPU. > **Notice:** Support for GPU upload heaps depends on hardware capabilities. It is available on systems with **integrated GPUs** or **discrete GPUs with full CPU access to GPU** memory (e.g., when *Resizable BAR* is enabled). On unsupported systems, the setting **has no effect**. | **Arguments:** **0** - disabled **1** - enabled (by default) |
| d3d12_memory_pool_heap_default |  |
| **Description:** - **Variable.**   Prints the current  default heap memory pool size, in megabytes, for allocations in GPU-local memory. - **Command.**   Sets the  default heap memory pool size, in megabytes, for allocations in GPU-local memory. | **Arguments:** **[0; 16384]** - available range **64** - by default |
| d3d12_memory_pool_heap_gpu_upload |  |
| **Description:** - **Variable.**   Prints the current  GPU upload heap memory pool size, in megabytes, for allocations used to upload data from system memory to GPU memory. - **Command.**   Sets the  GPU upload heap memory pool size, in megabytes, for allocations used to upload data from system memory to GPU memory. | **Arguments:** **[0; 16384]** - available range **16** - by default |
| d3d12_memory_pool_heap_readback |  |
| **Description:** - **Variable.**   Prints the current  readback heap memory pool size, in megabytes, for allocations used to read data back from GPU to system memory. - **Command.**   Sets the  readback heap memory pool size, in megabytes, for allocations used to read data back from GPU to system memory. | **Arguments:** **[0; 16384]** - available range **64** - by default |
| d3d12_memory_pool_heap_upload |  |
| **Description:** - **Variable.**   Prints the current  upload heap memory pool size, in megabytes, for upload allocations in system memory. - **Command.**   Sets the  upload heap memory pool size, in megabytes, for upload allocations in system memory. | **Arguments:** **[0; 16384]** - available range **8** - by default |
| d3d12_memory_pool_texture |  |
| **Description:** - **Variable.**   Prints the current  texture memory pool size, in megabytes, for texture allocations in GPU memory. - **Command.**   Sets the  texture memory pool size, in megabytes, for texture allocations in GPU memory. | **Arguments:** **[0; 16384]** - available range **128** - by default |
| d3d12_memory_pool_texture_staging |  |
| **Description:** - **Variable.**   Prints the current  staging texture memory pool size, in megabytes, for staging texture allocations in system memory. - **Command.**   Sets the  staging texture memory pool size, in megabytes, for staging texture allocations in system memory. | **Arguments:** **[0; 16384]** - available range **32** - by default |
| d3d12_frame_pool_upload |  |
| **Description:** - **Variable.**   Prints the current  current size of the CPU-visible frame upload pool used to allocate per-frame constant buffers and other transient data. - **Command.**   Sets the  current size of the CPU-visible frame upload pool used to allocate per-frame constant buffers and other transient data. | **Arguments:** **[0; 16384]** - available range **128** - by default |
| d3d12_frame_pool_gpu_upload |  |
| **Description:** - **Variable.**   Prints the current  current size of the GPU frame upload pool, which is used for per-frame allocations such as material constant buffers. - **Command.**   Sets the  current size of the GPU frame upload pool, which is used for per-frame allocations such as material constant buffers. | **Arguments:** **[0; 16384]** - available range **128** - by default |


#### Skinned Meshes and Decals Allocations


| skinned_pool_chunk_size |  |
|---|---|
| **Description:** - **Variable.**   Prints the current size of the VRAM chunk to be allocated within a separate pool for a skinned mesh. - **Command.**   Sets the size of the VRAM chunk to be allocated within a separate pool for a skinned mesh. Reducing the chunk size may negatively impact performance, since skinned geometry is processed more efficiently when it resides within a single chunk. | **Arguments:** **[4; 512]** - available range **64** - by default |
| decal_pool_chunk_size |  |
| **Description:** - **Variable.**   Prints the current size of the VRAM chunk to be allocated within a separate pool for a decal. - **Command.**   Sets the size of the VRAM chunk to be allocated within a separate pool for a decal. | **Arguments:** **[4; 512]** - available range **16** - by default |

## USC Scripts


Operations on the world, system and editor scripts.


### Editor Script Analyzer


Operations on the [editor script](../../code/fundamentals/execution_sequence/app_logic_system.md#editor_script) debugging.

> **Notice:** Available only for debug builds.


| editor_memory_usage |  |
|---|---|
| **Description:** - **Command.** Prints memory usage by the editor script to the console or dump into a specified file. | **Arguments:** `Path` to a file to dump the information into (optional) |
| editor_analyze |  |
| **Description:** - **Command.** Analyzes the performance of the editor script. The information can be printed to the console or dumped into a specified file. | **Arguments:** `Path` to the log file to dump the [log file](../../code/performance_analyzer.md) information into (optional) |
| editor_disassemble |  |
| **Description:** - **Command.** Disassembles the editor script. The information can be printed to the console or dumped into a specified file. | **Arguments:** `Path` to a file to dump the information into (optional) |

### Script Debugger


Operations on the per-function breakpoint. The syntax to set the breakpoint is the following:

```text
system_breakpoint/world_breakpoint/editor_breakpoint set/remove function_name number_of_arguments
```


| world_breakpoint |  |
|---|---|
| **Description:** - **Command.** Sets a [breakpoint](../../code/uniginescript/language/debugging.md#debugger_runtime) to the specified function in the world script. The syntax to set the breakpoint is the following: ```text world_breakpoint set/remove function_name number_of_arguments ``` | **Arguments:** 1. Name of **function** 2. **Number** of arguments |
| system_breakpoint |  |
| **Description:** - **Command.** Sets a [breakpoint](../../code/uniginescript/language/debugging.md#debugger_runtime) to the specified function in the system script. The syntax to set the breakpoint is the following: ```text system_breakpoint set/remove function_name number_of_arguments ``` | **Arguments:** 1. Name of **function** 2. **Number** of arguments |
| editor_breakpoint |  |
| **Description:** - **Command.** Set a [breakpoint](../../code/uniginescript/language/debugging.md#debugger_runtime) to the specified function in the editor script. The syntax to set the breakpoint is the following: ```text editor_breakpoint set/remove function_name number_of_arguments ``` | **Arguments:** 1. Name of **function** 2. **Number** of arguments |


## Miscellaneous


Miscellaneous commands.

| gpu_thread_priority |  |
|---|---|
| **Description:** - **Variable.**   Prints the current GPU thread priority for the engine. - **Command.**   Sets the GPU thread priority for the engine.  Available for DirectX only. Positive values increase the likelihood that the GPU scheduler will grant GPU execution cycles to the device when rendering. You should have a comprehensive understanding of GPU scheduling and profile your application to ensure that it behaves as intended. If used inappropriately, this parameter can impede rendering speed and result in a poor user experience. | **Arguments:** **[-7; 7]** - available range **7** - by default |
| process_priority | Config file: [*.boot](../../code/configuration_file_cpp.md#boot) |
| **Description:** - **Variable.**   Prints the current engine process priority. - **Command.**   Sets the engine process priority. Available for Windows only. A process with a higher priority gets to use the free CPU time available while a lower priority process only has access to the CPU when the higher priority application doesn't need it. If used inappropriately, may significantly affect performance. | **Arguments:** **0** - idle **1** - normal (by default) **2** - high **3** - real-time |
| log_stdout | Config file: [*.boot](../../code/configuration_file_cpp.md#boot) |
| **Description:** - **Variable.**   Prints a value indicating if the option controlled by the command below is enabled. - **Command.**   Enables log messages printing in stdout. > **Notice:** Logging to stdout may significantly affect performance, so switch this option off, when you don't need it. You can use [log_file](#log_file) for debugging purposes, as it is more performance-friendly. | **Arguments:** **0** - disabled **1** - enabled (by default) |
| log_file | Config file: [*.boot](../../code/configuration_file_cpp.md#boot) |
| **Description:** - **Variable.**   Prints a value indicating if the option controlled by the command below is enabled. - **Command.**   Enables log messages saving in the Engine's log file. > **Notice:** This option is used for debugging. Do not turn it off if you need to debug something. | **Arguments:** **0** - disabled **1** - enabled (by default) |
| dpi_awareness | Config file: [*.boot](../../code/configuration_file_cpp.md#boot) |
| **Description:** - **Variable.**   Prints the current DPI awareness mode, the value indicating how the application processes the DPI scaling. - **Command.**   Sets the DPI awareness mode, the value indicating how the application processes the DPI scaling. | **Arguments:** **-1** — user configures DPI awareness. **0** - all displays are default DPI, bitmap-stretching. **1** - all displays have the same DPI from primary display, bitmap-stretching. (by default) **2** - DPI of the display that the window is primarily located on, no DPI scaling of any UI elements. Not available on Linux. |
| auto_dpi_scaling |  |
| **Description:** - **Variable.**   Prints a value indicating if the option controlled by the command below is enabled. - **Command.**   Enables applying automatic scaling to the window content. | **Arguments:** **0** - disabled **1** - enabled (by default) |
| swap_delay_warning | Config file: [*.boot](../../code/configuration_file_cpp.md#boot) |
| **Description:** - **Variable.**   Prints a value indicating if the option controlled by the command below is enabled. - **Command.**   Enables displaying of the warning to the console that the swap has not been called within the period specified by [swap_delay_warning_time](#swap_delay_warning_time). | **Arguments:** **0** - disabled (by default) **1** - enabled |
| swap_delay_warning_time | Config file: [*.boot](../../code/configuration_file_cpp.md#boot) |
| **Description:** - **Variable.**   Prints the current time in milliseconds, during which the swap should be called, otherwise [swap_delay_warning](#swap_delay_warning) is displayed in the console. - **Command.**   Sets the time in milliseconds, during which the swap should be called, otherwise [swap_delay_warning](#swap_delay_warning) is displayed in the console. | **Arguments:** **[1.0; 1000000.0]** - available range **200.0** - by default |
| license_info |  |
| **Description:** Prints license information on all third-party libraries used. |  |
